#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_activities
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_activities;

CREATE TABLE `bf_activities` (
  `activity_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `activity` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `module` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`activity_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=136 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_catalog_itemparams
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_catalog_itemparams;

CREATE TABLE `bf_catalog_itemparams` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `catalog_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `param_type` char(10) NOT NULL,
  `fldformtype` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `value` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_record_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extra_data` text NOT NULL,
  `pos` tinyint(3) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `hidden` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `recfile_id` bigint(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `catalog_id` (`catalog_id`),
  KEY `name` (`name`),
  KEY `extformtable_id` (`extformtable_id`),
  KEY `extformtable_record_id` (`extformtable_record_id`),
  KEY `fldformtype` (`fldformtype`),
  KEY `pos` (`pos`),
  KEY `hidden` (`hidden`),
  KEY `deleted` (`deleted`),
  KEY `recfile_id` (`recfile_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `bf_catalog_itemparams_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`catalog_id`) REFERENCES `bf_catalogs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=7 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_catalog_items;

CREATE TABLE `bf_catalog_items` (
  `id` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `descr` text NOT NULL,
  `hidden` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,

  `date_created` datetime NOT NULL,

  KEY `catalog_id` (`catalog_id`),

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=59 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_catalog_itemvalues
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_catalog_itemvalues;

CREATE TABLE `bf_catalog_itemvalues` (
  `id` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `item_id` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `itemparam_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `itemvalue` text NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_record_id` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `recfile_id` bigint(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `itemparam_id` (`itemparam_id`),
  KEY `item_id` (`item_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `bf_catalog_itemvalues_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`itemparam_id`) REFERENCES `bf_catalog_itemparams` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `bf_catalog_itemvalues_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`item_id`) REFERENCES `bf_catalog_items` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=54 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_catalog_params
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_catalog_params;

CREATE TABLE `bf_catalog_params` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `catalog_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `param_type` char(10) NOT NULL,
  `fldformtype` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `value` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extformtable_record_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `extra_data` text NOT NULL,
  `pos` tinyint(3) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `hidden` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `recfile_id` bigint(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `catalog_id` (`catalog_id`),
  KEY `name` (`name`),
  KEY `extformtable_id` (`extformtable_id`),
  KEY `extformtable_record_id` (`extformtable_record_id`),
  KEY `fldformtype` (`fldformtype`),
  KEY `pos` (`pos`),
  KEY `hidden` (`hidden`),
  KEY `deleted` (`deleted`),
  KEY `recfile_id` (`recfile_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `bf_catalog_params_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`catalog_id`) REFERENCES `bf_catalogs` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE ON UPDATE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=14 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_catalog_params (`id`, `catalog_id`, `name`, `title`, `param_type`, `fldformtype`, `value`, `extformtable_id`, `extformtable_record_id`, `extra_data`, `pos`, `hidden`, `deleted`, `recfile_id`) VALUES (7, 19, 'kassetetype', 'Тип кассеты', 'extform', '', '3', 17, 3, '', 3, 0, 0, 0);

  KEY `extformtable_id` (`extformtable_id`),
  KEY `extformtable_record_id` (`extformtable_record_id`),
  KEY `ds_type` (`ds_type`),
  KEY `pos` (`pos`),
  KEY `name` (`name`),
  KEY `catalog_id` (`catalog_id`,`item_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=23 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=5 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_email_queue
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_email_queue;

CREATE TABLE `bf_email_queue` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `to_email` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `subject` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `message` text NOT NULL,
  `alt_message` text,
  `max_attempts` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '3',
  `attempts` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `success` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `date_published` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_attempt` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `date_sent` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_extformtables
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_extformtables;

CREATE TABLE `bf_extformtables` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `fullname` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `noprefix` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `name` (`name`,`title`),
  KEY `fullname` (`fullname`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=20 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

Ответственность за взрывы взяла на себя нигерийская исламистская террористическая группировка <em>\"Боко Харам\"</em>.</span> <a class=\"source\" href=\"http://www.interfax.ru/society/news.asp?id=223713\" target=\"_blank\">Интерфакс</a> <span class=\"time\">&nbsp;16:52</span></p>\r\n<p class=\"text\"><span>В результате пяти взрывов, совершенных в Рождественское воскресенье у христианских церквей в различных городах Нигерии, погибли, по меньшей мере, 25 человек.   `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,

  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `name` (`name`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=4 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_inforecords
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_inforecords;

CREATE TABLE `bf_inforecords` (
  `id` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `table_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `hidden` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `group_id` int(10) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `table_id` (`table_id`),
  KEY `group_id` (`group_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_inforecordvalues
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_inforecordvalues;

CREATE TABLE `bf_inforecordvalues` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `param_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `table_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `record_id` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `charvalue` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `textvalue` text NOT NULL,
  `intvalue` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `bigtextvalue` longtext NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `param_id` (`param_id`),
  KEY `table_id` (`table_id`),
  KEY `charvalue` (`charvalue`),
  KEY `intvalue` (`intvalue`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_reports
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_reports;

CREATE TABLE `bf_reports` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `sysname` varchar(20) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `active` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=9 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_roles
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_roles;

CREATE TABLE `bf_roles` (
  `role_id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `role_name` varchar(60) NOT NULL,
  `description` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `default` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `can_delete` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `login_destination` varchar(255) NOT NULL DEFAULT '/',
  `deleted` int(1) DEFAULT '0',
  PRIMARY KEY (`role_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=7 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_schema_version
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_schema_version;

CREATE TABLE `bf_schema_version` (
  `version` int(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `app_version` int(4) DEFAULT '0',
  `news_version` int(4) DEFAULT '0'
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

INSERT INTO bf_schema_version (`version`, `app_version`, `news_version`) VALUES (8, 0, 1);


#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_sessions
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_sessions;

CREATE TABLE `bf_sessions` (
  `session_id` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `ip_address` varchar(16) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `user_agent` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `last_activity` int(10) unsigned NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `user_data` text,
  PRIMARY KEY (`session_id`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_tpls
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_tpls;

CREATE TABLE `bf_tpls` (
  `id` int(10) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `title` varchar(255) NOT NULL,
  `tpl` text NOT NULL,
  `modified` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  `active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  `opt` tinyint(1) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `name` (`name`),
  KEY `modified` (`modified`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=7 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_user_cookies
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_user_cookies;

CREATE TABLE `bf_user_cookies` (
  `user_id` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(128) NOT NULL,
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL,
  KEY `token` (`token`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;

#
# TABLE STRUCTURE FOR: bf_users
#

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS bf_users;

CREATE TABLE `bf_users` (
  `id` bigint(20) unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `role_id` int(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '4',
  `first_name` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `last_name` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(120) NOT NULL,
  `username` varchar(30) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `password_hash` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `reset_hash` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `salt` varchar(7) NOT NULL,
  `last_login` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `last_ip` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
  `created_on` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT '0000-00-00 00:00:00',
  `street_1` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `street_2` varchar(255) DEFAULT NULL,
  `city` varchar(40) DEFAULT NULL,
  `zipcode` varchar(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `reset_by` int(10) DEFAULT NULL,
  `country_iso` char(2) DEFAULT 'US',
  `state_code` char(4) DEFAULT '',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `email` (`email`)
) ENGINE=MyISAM AUTO_INCREMENT=6 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8;
